  <script type="text/javascript">
   /**
		 * Makes an ajax request to change the current course, then refreshes the page
		 */	
		function goToCourse( courseID ){
			//alert (courseID);
			if ( courseID === "top" ) {
				var subSessInd = document.URL.indexOf("." + global_subsessionID);
				if (subSessInd == -1)
				{ 
					window.location.href = getURLForCurrentSession("student" + global_urlDelim + "top");
				} else {
					var url  = document.URL.substring(0, subSessInd);
					url += "." + global_subsessionID + global_urlDelim + "student" + global_urlDelim + "top";
					window.location = url;
				}
			} else {
				ajax("student",'ajax/course/changeCourse.php','','',false,'changeCourse',courseID, 
					function(){//On success
						// Refresh the page
						if ( global_viewID == 'top')
						{
							var baseUrl = ".sXi9/cid-0yOoxjcvQSwI/student/home";
							var subSessInd = document.URL.indexOf("." + global_subsessionID);
							var pageUrl = "";
							if (subSessInd == -1)
							{ 
								pageUrl = baseUrl.replace(global_subsessionID + global_urlDelim, global_subsessionID + global_urlDelim + "cid-" + courseID + global_urlDelim);
							} else {
								pageUrl = document.URL.substring(0, subSessInd) + baseUrl;
							}
							window.location = pageUrl;
						} 
						else 
						{ 														var url = document.URL.replace("cid-" + global_courseID + global_urlDelim, "cid-" + courseID + global_urlDelim);								url = url.replace(/\/id-[0-9A-Za-z_\-]{4}/, '');										window.location = url;
						}
				}, function() {//On error
						showAlert("error", {txt: "There was an error loading the course."});
				});
			}
			
			return false;
		};

		/**
		 * Makes an ajax request to change the current course, then refreshes the page
		 */
		function changeCourseStudent( courseID, stopVerify, redirect ){
			var redirectUrl = redirect ? redirect : window.location;

			console.log('courseID: ' + courseID);
			console.log('redirect: ' + redirect);

				// Nulling out the course on our way to the top app
				courseID = null;
				redirectUrl = '.sXi9/student/top';
			}

			// this is not working
			ajax('student', 'ajax/course/changeCourse.php', '', '', true, 'changeCourse', courseID, function(e){
				window.location = redirectUrl;
			}, function(error){
				console.log(error);
			});
		};

				window.location = href;
			});
		}

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function renderPlagiarismElement( overlapPercentage ) {
                if (overlapPercentage < 0)
                    return "No Data";
                else {
                    var similarityLink = "<span class='plagiarism-text'>" +overlapPercentage+"%</span><span class='plagiarism plagiarism-";

                    if(overlapPercentage == 0){
                        similarityLink += "blue";
                    }
                    else if(overlapPercentage <= 24){
                        similarityLink += "green";
                    }
                    else if(overlapPercentage <= 49){
                        similarityLink += "yellow";
                    }
                    else if(overlapPercentage <= 74){
                        similarityLink += "orange";
                    }
                    else{
                        similarityLink += "red";
                    }
                    similarityLink += "' title='" + overlapPercentage + "%'></span>";
                    return similarityLink;
                }
            }
  </script>

  <!-- datepicker.php -->
  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(document).ready( function() {
				$(".datepicker").prop('readonly', true).datepicker();
			});
			
			// DatePicker object
			function DatePicker(id, options) {				
				if(id.substring && id.length > 0 ) {
					if( $('#'+id).length == 0 ) {
						throw "Failed to make DatePicker from element with "
							+"id = '"+id+"'. No DOM element found.";
					} else if( $('#'+id).length > 1 ) {
						throw "Failed to make DatePicker from element with "
							+"id = '"+id+"'. Multiple DOM elements found.";
					} else if( !$('#'+id).is('input') ) {
						throw "Failed to make DatePicker from element with "
							+"id =' "+id+"'. DatePickers can only be created from <input> elements.";
					}
					
					this.id = id;
					if(!options) {
						options = {limit : DatePicker.limit.none};
					}
					this.config = options;
					DatePicker.config[id] = options;
					
					$('#'+id).addClass('datepicker').prop('readonly', true).datepicker();
				} else {
					throw "Failed to make DatePicker. Invalid id '"+id+"' given.";
				}
			}	 
			
			/** instance getter */
			DatePicker.prototype.getValue = function() {
				return DatePicker.getValue(this.id);
			}
			
			/** instance setter */
			DatePicker.prototype.setValue = function(value) {
				DatePicker.setValue(this.id, value);
			}
			
			/** static getter */
			DatePicker.getValue = function(id) {
				var value = $('#'+id).val();
				if( value.length > 0 ) {
					var date = Date.parse(value, "MM/dd/yyyy");
					return date.toString('yyyy-MM-dd');
				} 
				return value;
			}
			
			/** static setter */
			DatePicker.setValue = function(id, value) {
				if(value) {
					var date = Date.parse(value, "yyyy-MM-dd");
					if( date ) {
						$('#'+id).val( date.toString('M/d/yyyy') );
					}
				} else {
					$('#'+id).val('');
				}
			}
			
			/**
			 * Converts a date string formatted yyyy-MM-dd to one formatted M/d/yyyy
			 */
			DatePicker.changeDateToUserFormat = function( date ){
				var date = Date.parse(date, "yyyy-MM-dd");
				return date.toString('M/d/yyyy');
			}
			
			/**
			 * Converts a date string formatted MM/dd/yyyy to one formatted yyyy-MM-dd
			 */
			DatePicker.changeDateFromUserFormat = function( date ){
				var date = Date.parse(date, "MM/dd/yyyy");
				return date.toString('yyyy-MM-dd');
			}
			
			DatePicker.firstDayOfPeriod = global_firstDayOfPeriod;DatePicker.lastDayOfPeriod = global_lastDayOfPeriod; 			
			DatePicker.util = function(){};
			
			/**
			 * Ensures that the DatePicker.lastDayOfPeriod is always the max of the CalendarDays
			 * or 10 days after the end of classes.
			 */
			DatePicker.util.adjustPeriodEndForFinals = function() {
				// Tom asked that we extend the end by 10 days so that we can get finals week in
				
				var globalLastDay = Date.parse(global_lastDayOfPeriod);
				globalLastDay.addDays(10);
				var localLastDay = Date.parse(DatePicker.lastDayOfPeriod);
				
				DatePicker.lastDayOfPeriod = globalLastDay.toString('M/d/yyyy');
				if( localLastDay.isAfter(globalLastDay) ) {
					DatePicker.lastDayOfPeriod = localLastDay.toString('M/d/yyyy');
				}
			}
			
			DatePicker.util.adjustPeriodEndForFinals();
			
			// Static constants
			DatePicker.limit = function(){};
			DatePicker.limit.none = "none";
			DatePicker.limit.period = "period";
			DatePicker.limit.range = "range";
			
			// Config options for all DatePicker instances on the page
			DatePicker.config = [];
						
			function getDatePickerContent(id){
				return DatePicker.getValue(id);
			}
						
			function setDatePickerContent(id, value){
				DatePicker.setValue(id, value);
			}

			/**
			 * Converts a date string formatted yyyy-MM-dd to one formatted M/d/yyyy
			 */
			function changeDateToUserFormat( date ){
				DatePicker.changeDateToUserFormat(date);
			}

			/**
			 * Converts a date string formatted MM/dd/yyyy to one formatted yyyy-MM-dd
			 */
			function changeDateFromUserFormat( date ){
				DatePicker.changeDateFromUserFormat(date);
			}
			
			/**
			 * Will change the Javascript cached period start and period end variables
			 * if the dateString is outside the period
			 * @param dateString The string date representation
			 * @return True if a cached period date was changed, otherwise False
			 */
			DatePicker.extendCachedPeriod = function(dateString) {
				var newDate = Date.parse(dateString);
				var periodStart = Date.parse(DatePicker.firstDayOfPeriod);
				
				if( newDate.isBefore(periodStart) ) {
					DatePicker.firstDayOfPeriod = newDate.toString("MM/dd/yyyy");
					return true;
				} else {
					var periodEnd = Date.parse(DatePicker.lastDayOfPeriod);
					if( newDate.isAfter(periodEnd) ) {
						DatePicker.lastDayOfPeriod = newDate.toString("MM/dd/yyyy");
						DatePicker.util.adjustPeriodEndForFinals();
						return true;
					}
				}
				
				return false;
			}
			
			/**
			 * Static Method. Asynchronously queries for the most recent period start 
			 * and end and updates DatePicker variables as needed. 
			 */
			DatePicker.updatePeriodRange = function() {
				ajax(global_appID, 
					"ajax/controls/datepicker.php", 
					'', '', false, 
					'getPeriodRange', ['nothing'], 
					function(data){ /* success */
						try {
							var result = $.parseJSON(data);
							if( !DatePicker.extendCachedPeriod(result.start) ) {
								// Shortening the range, but do not shorten beyond global_firstDayOfPeriod
								var periodStart = Date.parse(global_firstDayOfPeriod);
								var newStart = Date.parse(result.start);
								
								if( newStart.isAfter(periodStart) ) {
									DatePicker.firstDayOfPeriod = newStart.toString("MM/dd/yyyy");
								} else {
									DatePicker.firstDayOfPeriod = periodStart.toString("MM/dd/yyyy");
								}
							}
							
							if( !DatePicker.extendCachedPeriod(result.end) ) {
								// Shortening the range, but do not shorten beyond global_lastDayOfPeriod
								var periodEnd = Date.parse(global_lastDayOfPeriod);
								var newEnd = Date.parse(result.end);
								
								if( newEnd.isAfter(periodEnd) ) {
									DatePicker.lastDayOfPeriod = newEnd.toString("MM/dd/yyyy");
								} else {
									DatePicker.lastDayOfPeriod = periodEnd.toString("MM/dd/yyyy");
								}
							}
							
							DatePicker.util.adjustPeriodEndForFinals();
						} catch(e) {
							console.log('Failed to update the period range for DatePicker.');
						}
					}, 
					function(ajaxObj){ /* failure */
						console.log('Failed to update the period range for DatePicker. '+ajaxObj.responseText);
					});
			}
  </script>

					placement = 'bottom';

				{
					placement = 'right';
				}
				else //the placement is fine where it's at
				{
					return;

				$('#showCHID').popover('destroy');

			$('body').on('click', 'a,div,span', function(e) {
				if(!$(e.target).parents('.popover').length) {
					if(!$(e.target).is("#showCHID")) {
						$('#showCHID').popover('hide');
					}
					if($(e.target).is(".stats-disallowed") || $(e.target).parents('.stats-disallowed').length) {
						var $target;
					if($(e.target).is(".stats-disallowed")) {
							$target = $(e.target);
						} else {
							$target = $(e.target).parents('.stats-disallowed');
						}
						var isShowing = $target.data('popover').tip().hasClass('in');
						$('.stats-disallowed').popover('hide');
						if(isShowing) {
							$target.popover('show');
						} else {
							$target.popover('hide');
						}
					} else {
						$('.stats-disallowed').popover('hide');
					}
				}
				if (e.target.tagName.toLowerCase() != "a")
				{
					return;
				}
				if ( e.target.href != undefined && e.target.href.indexOf("#") == -1 )
				{
					return true;		//If it is a valid href, with no # send it through.
				} else {
					return false;
				}
				
			});

                {{#wrongOS}}
                <p>Note that you may need to install additional software to play this type of video file</p>
                {{/wrongOS}}
            </div>
  </script>
  <!-- MediaPopup -->
  <script type="text/javascript">
   var MAXHEIGHT = document.documentElement.clientHeight / 100 * 70;
            var MAXWIDTH = document.documentElement.clientHeight / 100 * 70;

            var HUMAN_READABLE_FILETYPES = {
                'video/mpeg': 'MPEG or MPG',
                'video/avi': 'AVI',
                'video/aif': 'AIF',
                'video/aiff': 'AIFF',
                'video/mp4': 'MP4',
                'video/x-flv': 'FLV (Flash Video)',
                'video/mov': "MOV",
                'video/wmv': "WMV",
                'video/webm': "WebM",
                'audio/mp3': "MP3",
                'audio/wma': "WMA",
                'audio/wav': 'WAV',
                'audio/aif': "AIF",
                'audio/aiff': "AIFF",
                'video/x-m4v': "M4V"
            };

            var HUMAN_READABLE_BROWSERS = {
                'msie': "Internet Explorer",
                'chrome': "Chrome",
                'firefox': "Firefox",
                'safari': "Safari",
                'opera': "Opera"
            };


            // Popup setup
            $('#mediaViewer').LSPopup({center:true, linkCloseFunctionToModal: false, closeFunction:closeMedia}).removeClass('hidden');

			            $(document).ready(function(){
                $(".downloadFile").click(function(){
                    //Pause video before we start downloading the file
                    if($('#mediaViewer div.mediaContent').find('audio,video').length > 0) {
						var player = new MediaElementPlayer($('#mediaViewer div.mediaContent').find('audio,video').selector);
					
						//Handle both the new and old player
						if ( !player.media )
						{
							player = new MediaElementPlayer($('#mediaViewer div.mediaContent').find('audio,video')[0]);
						}
                        player.pause();
                    }

                    var href = $('#downloadFileId').attr("mediaSrc");
                    window.open(href+"&download=true");
                });
            });
						
            function closeMedia() {
                // Trying pausing the media first, FF let audio keep playing
                if($('#mediaViewer div.mediaContent').find('audio,video').length > 0) {
                    var player = new MediaElementPlayer($('#mediaViewer div.mediaContent').find('audio,video').selector);
					
					//Handle both the new and old player
					if ( !player.media )
					{
						player = new MediaElementPlayer($('#mediaViewer div.mediaContent').find('audio,video')[0]);
					}
					
                    player.pause();
                    player.remove();
					
					//Handle both the new and old player
					if ( typeof mejs.players.indexOf === "function" )
					{
						// There is no destroy method, so players build up.  This removes them so they are no longer referenced.
						var index = mejs.players.indexOf(player);
						if(index >= 0) {
							mejs.players.splice(index, 1);
						}
					}
                }

                $('#mediaViewer div.mediaContent').html('<div id="replaceMeWithMedia"></div>');
                $('#mediaViewer').css('max-width', 'none');
                $('#mediaViewer').LSPopupClose();
            }

            /* Onclick event for media images to display the file
                */
            $(document).delegate('.media_Video, .media_Audio', 'click', function(event){
                showMedia($(this));
            });

            $(document).delegate('.media_Flash', 'click', function(event){
                embedFlash($(this));
            });

            /**
                * Embeds flash in the popup
                * @param link The visible <a> that represents the flash to embed
                */
            function embedFlash ( link ) {
                var src = link.attr( 'mediaSrc' );
                if ( src != '' ) {
                    var height = link.attr( 'hght' );
                    var width = link.attr( 'wdth' );
                    if ( width > MAXWIDTH ) {
                        height = ( MAXWIDTH / width ) * height ;
                        width = MAXWIDTH;
                    }

                    if ( height > MAXHEIGHT ) { // if height still exceeds 480
                        width = ( MAXHEIGHT / height ) * width ;
                        height = MAXHEIGHT;
                    }
					//So the .swf can be downloaded
					$( '#downloadFileId' ).attr( 'mediaSrc', src );
					
                    swfobject.embedSWF( src, "replaceMeWithMedia", width, height, "9.0.0",
                        "plugins/controls/swfobject/expressInstall.swf", {}, {wmode:"transparent"});
                    changeLSPopupTitle( "mediaViewer", "Flash" );
                    $( '#mediaViewer' ).removeClass( 'hidden' ).LSPopupOpen();

                    // Chrome sometimes does not redraw the <object> space,
                    // so this was a fix I found to trigger a redraw
                    var content = $( 'div.mediaContent' ).children().get(0);
                    if ( content.style && content.style.webkitTransform != undefined ) {
                        content.style.webkitTransform = 'scale(1)';
                    }
                }
            }

            /**
                * Creates the appropriate media element from the given media url and displays
                * it in the popup
                * @param image The visible image that represents the embeded media
                */
            function showMedia ( image ) {
                //Get information on the file to pass to GetID3 to find the codec
                var filepath = $( image ).attr( 'mediasrc' );
                //Regex to get FileID from filepath
                var fileIDregex = new RegExp( "fileId=(.[^&]*)", "i" ); //stops before "&" if SCOUT ID
                //Get fileID from file path
                var fileID = fileIDregex.exec( filepath )[1];
                //Check filepath to see if file is from SCOUT
                var fromScout = false;
                if ( filepath.match( /service=scout/ ) ) {
                    fromScout = true;
                }

                                //ajax call to use GetID3 to find audio/video codecs
                $( "body" ).css( "cursor", "progress" );
                ajax('gradebook', // The file belongs the current application
                'controls/MediaPopup.php', // Path relative to includes directory
                'MediaPopup', // This is in the MediaPopup class
                'none', // Param for MediaPopup constructor function
                false, // Not a page
                'getCodecs', // Call this function
                { fileID: fileID, fromScout: fromScout }, // fileID to pass in, and if from SCOUT
                     function ( result ) {
                    //console.log(result);
                    var codecs = JSON.parse( result );
                    $( "body" ).css( "cursor", "auto" );
                    if (image.attr("mime") == "video/mov" && codecs && codecs["video"] && codecs["video"] == "avc1")
                    {	//Specific case that will get modern apple movies working - may not need this after updating mediaplayer.
                        image.attr("mime", "video/mp4");
                    }
                    showMedia2( image, codecs );
                }, function () {//ERROR
                    $( "body" ).css( "cursor", "auto" );
                    console.log( 'getCodecs error' );
                });
            }


            /**
                * Second half of showMedia() function listed above
                * This is called after the ajax call returns with the codecs
                *
                * @param image The visible image that represents the embeded media
                * @param codecs Associative array containing video and audio codecs
                */
            function showMedia2 ( image, codecs ) {
                //Create a video test element, to see if the browser can play a video with
                //the given type and codec of the video we're trying to play
                var testEl = document.createElement( "video" );
                var mimeType = $( image ).attr( 'mime' );
                var playableVideo;

                //Check if QuickTime is installed
                var haveqt = checkQuickTimeInstalled();

                if ( testEl.canPlayType ) {
                    //Test mimetype and codec to see if it can be played (it will be "probably", "maybe", or "I don't know")
                    //NOTE: This method can only return "probably" if codec information is given
                    playableVideo = testEl.canPlayType( mimeType + ";codecs=" + codecs['video'] );
                }

                //If videos are h264, webm, or ogg, additionally test with Modernizr (Modernizr supported video tests)
                if ( codecs['video'].match( /h([. -])?264/gi ) && playableVideo != "probably"
                        && ( mimeType != "video/mov" && haveqt ) ) { //if h264 .mov file and QuickTime is installed, we'll play through there
                    playableVideo = Modernizr.video.h264;
                }
                if ( mimeType.match( /webm/gi ) && playableVideo != "probably" ) {
                    playableVideo = Modernizr.video.webm;
                }
                if ( mimeType.match( /video\/ogg/gi ) && playableVideo != "probably" ) {
                    playableVideo = Modernizr.video.ogg;
                }

                //If playableVideo hasn't returned 'probably', and QuickTime plugin is installed, check Quicktime compatibility
                if ( playableVideo != "probably" && haveqt ) {
                    playableVideo = checkQuickTimeSupport( mimeType, codecs['video'] );
                    if ( playableVideo == "probably" ) {
                        $(image).attr( 'mediaType', 'QuickTime' );
                    }
                }

                //For flash video types, detect if flash is enabled, and set playableVideo to "probably" if it is
                //(code from here: https://stackoverflow.com/questions/998245/how-can-i-detect-if-flash-is-installed-and-if-not-display-a-hidden-div-that-inf)
                if ( mimeType.match( /x-flv/gi ) ) {
                    var hasFlash = checkFlashInstalled();
                    if ( hasFlash ) {
                        playableVideo = "probably";
                    }
                }

                //Similar to above, but with an audio test element
                var testEl2 = document.createElement( "audio" );
                var playableAudio;
                if ( testEl2.canPlayType ) {
                    playableAudio = testEl2.canPlayType(mimeType + ";codecs=" + codecs['audio']);
                }

                //If audio is ogg, mp3, wav, or m4a, additionally test with Modernizr (Modernizr supported audio tests)
                if ( mimeType.match( /audio\/ogg/gi ) && playableAudio != "probably" ) {
                    playableAudio = Modernizr.audio.ogg;
                }
                if ( mimeType.match( /mp3/gi ) && playableAudio != "probably" ) {
                    playableAudio = Modernizr.audio.mp3;
                }
                if ( mimeType.match( /wav/gi ) && playableAudio != "probably" ) {
                    playableAudio = Modernizr.audio.wav;
                }
                if ( mimeType.match( /m4a/gi ) && playableAudio != "probably" ) {
                    playableAudio = Modernizr.audio.m4a;
                }

                var itemId = $( image ).attr( 'mediaSrc' );
                $( '#downloadFileId' ).attr( 'mediaSrc', itemId );

                //Detect browser and os - currently only used for error message to display if
                //file type can't be played
                var browser = browserDetect(); //Sniff used browser
                var os = operatingSystemDetect(); //Sniff used OS

                //Use either playableAudio (for audio files) or playableVideo (for video files)
                //to determine whether media type can be played.
                //Also set fileCodec to be displayed if error popup is shown.
                var mediaType = $( image ).attr( 'media' );
                var fileCodec;
                var playableMedia;
                if ( mediaType == "audio" ) {
                    playableMedia = playableAudio;
                    fileCodec = codecs['audio'];
                }
                else if ( mediaType == "video" ) {
                    playableMedia = playableVideo;
                    fileCodec = codecs['video'];
                }


        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

            // THIS LINE COMPLETELY IGNORES THE ABOVE CHECKS AND TRIES TO PLAY NO MATTER WHAT. It was
            // decided that these checks were being too harsh (not allowing videos to play that people
            // thought should be able to), so now we'll just attempt to play anything.

            // NOTE: In the testing I did when originally implementing this, I never found a video that
            // failed the above checks but could actually play in the browser. So this may just break
            // the video player.

                playableMedia = "probably"; //force all video and audio to play

        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

                if ( playableMedia == "probably" ) {
                    var media = createMediaElement( image );
                    if( media != null ) {
                        $( '#mediaViewer div.mediaContent' ).html( media );
                    } else {
                        $( '#mediaViewer div.mediaContent' ).html( 'Sorry. We do not support this media type' );
                    }
                        playCurrentMedia();

                }
                else {
                    changeLSPopupTitle( "mediaViewer", "Media" );
                    var unsupportedMimeElement = renderUnsupportedFileTypeElement( browser, os, $( image ).attr( 'mime' ), fileCodec );
                    $( '#mediaViewer div.mediaContent' ).html( unsupportedMimeElement );
                    $( '#mediaViewer' ).css( 'max-width', '550px' );
                }

                $('#mediaViewer').removeClass('hidden').LSPopupOpen();
            }

            /**
                * Renders an explanation for the media popup that the given audio or video type isn't supported
                *      by the preview player.
                */
            function renderUnsupportedFileTypeElement ( userBrowser, userOs, userFileType, fileCodec ) {
                //Set Browser type for template message
                var readableBrowser = HUMAN_READABLE_BROWSERS[userBrowser];
                if(readableBrowser == undefined){
                    readableBrowser = "unknown";
                }
                if ( fileCodec == "" ) {
                    fileCodec = "unknown";
                }

                //Set File Type for template message
                var readableFileType = (HUMAN_READABLE_FILETYPES[userFileType] == undefined ? userFileType : HUMAN_READABLE_FILETYPES[userFileType]);

                //Create initial template data object
                var templateData = {
                    browser: readableBrowser,
                    os: userOs,
                    fileType: readableFileType,
                    codec: fileCodec
                };

                //Determine whether any special OS codec issues apply
                if ( userOs == "MacOS" ) {
                    if ( userFileType == 'video/wmv' )
                        templateData.wrongOS = true;
                }
                else if ( userOs == "Windows" ) {
                    if ( userFileType == "audio/aiff" || userFileType == "audio/aif" )
                        templateData.wrongOS = true;
                }

                //Determine whether is an audio or video file
                if ( strstr( userFileType, 'audio' ) != false ) {
                    templateData.audioFile = true;
                    templateData.mediaType = 'audio';
                    templateData.headerMediaType = "Audio";
                }
                else if ( strstr( userFileType, 'video' ) != false ) {
                    templateData.videoFile = true;
                    templateData.mediaType = 'video';
                    templateData.headerMediaType = "Video";
                }

                var template = $( "#mpCantPlayDialog" ).html();
                var compiledTemplate = Hogan.compile( template );
                var output = compiledTemplate.render( templateData );

                return output;
            }

            /**
                * Extracts the file type from the media url
                * @param src The url for the media file
                * @returns The file type (mp4, mp3, etc) of the media file
                */
            function getFileType ( src ) {
                var strArr = src.split( '.' );
                return strArr[strArr.length - 1];
            }

            /**
                * Generates the HTML for various media types. Returns null if the type
                * is not recognized.
                * @param image The visible image that represents the embeded media
                * @returns The HTML for the media or null
                */
            function createMediaElement ( image ) {
                var media = $( image ).attr( 'media' );
                if ( media == 'audio' ) {
                    changeLSPopupTitle( "mediaViewer", "Audio" );
                    return createAudioElement( image );
                } else {
                    changeLSPopupTitle( "mediaViewer", "Video" );
                    return createVideoElement( image );
                }
            }

            /**
                * Checks if Flash is installed in the browser
                * (code from here: https://stackoverflow.com/questions/998245/how-can-i-detect-if-flash-is-installed-and-if-not-display-a-hidden-div-that-inf)
                * @return hasFlash (bool) if Flash is installed
                */
            function checkFlashInstalled(){
                var hasFlash = false;
                try {
                    var fo = new ActiveXObject( 'ShockwaveFlash.ShockwaveFlash' );
                    if ( fo ) {
                        hasFlash = true;
                    }
                } catch ( e ) {
                    if ( navigator.mimeTypes
                            && navigator.mimeTypes['application/x-shockwave-flash'] != undefined
                            && navigator.mimeTypes['application/x-shockwave-flash'].enabledPlugin ) {
                        hasFlash = true;
                    }
                }
                return hasFlash;
            }

            /**
                * Checks if QuickTime is installed in the browser
                * @return haveqt (bool) if QuickTime is installed
                */
            function checkQuickTimeInstalled () {
                var haveqt = false;

                //Check for QuickTime plugin
                if ( navigator.plugins ) {
                    for ( var i=0; i < navigator.plugins.length; i++ ) {
                        if ( navigator.plugins[i].name.indexOf("QuickTime") >= 0 ) {
                            haveqt = true;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }

                if ( (navigator.appVersion.indexOf("Mac") > 0 )
                        && ( navigator.appName.substring(0,9) == "Microsoft" )
                        && ( parseInt( navigator.appVersion ) < 5) ) {
                    haveqt = true;
                }

                return haveqt;
            }


            /**
                * Checks if video MIME type and codec are compatible with the QuickTime player
                * @param fileType the MIME type of the video file
                * @param videoCodec the video codec
                * @returns "probably" or ""
                */
            function checkQuickTimeSupport( fileType, videoCodec ) {
                    var rightType = false;
                    var rightCodec = false;
                    var playableVideo = "";
                    //QuickTime supported MIME types
                    var qtFileTypes = [ "video/mov", "video/mp4", "video/x-m4v", "video/mpeg", "video/avi" ];
                    //Quicktime supported codecs (initial list copied from here http://www.simnet.is/klipklap/quicktime/)
                    var qtCodecs = [ "Animation", "Apple ProRes 4444", "BMP (Apple BMP)", "Cinepak", "Component Video", "DV PAL/NTSC",
                        "DVCPRO PAL/NTSC", "Graphics", "H.261", "H.263", "H.264", "Intel Indeo 5", "Intel Raw", "JPEG 2000", "Microsoft OLE",
                        "Microsoft RLE", "Microsoft Video 1 (CRAM)", "Motion-JPEG A", "Motion-JPEG B", "mp4v", "MPEG-1", "MPEG-2", "MPEG-4",
                        "Photo - JPEG", "Pixlet", "Planar RGB", "PNG", "Radius Cinepak", "Sorenson Video", "Sorenson Video (rev.2)",
                        "Sorenson Video 3", "TGA", "TIFF", "Video (Apple Video)" ];

                    //Check against supported QuickTime MIME types
                    for ( var i = 0; i < qtFileTypes.length; i++ ) {
                        if ( fileType === qtFileTypes[i] ) {
                            rightType = true;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                    //Check against supported QuickTime codecs
                    for ( var i = 0; i < qtCodecs.length; i++ ) {
                        if ( videoCodec === qtCodecs[i] ) {
                            rightCodec = true;
                            break;
                        }
                    }

                    //For now, let through any videos with the right type OR right codec.  This may let through videos that can't
                    //actually be played, and we may change this later.
                    if ( rightType || rightCodec ) {
                        playableVideo = "probably";
                    }

                return playableVideo;

            }

            /**
                * Generates the HTML for various video file types. Returns null if the
                * format is not recognized.
                * @param image The visible image that represents the embeded media
                * @returns The HTML for the video or null
                */
            function createVideoElement ( image ) {
                var src = $( image ).attr( 'mediaSrc' );
                src += '&downloadType=stream';
                var vidType = $( image ).attr( 'mediaType' );
                if( vidType == 'file' || vidType == 'QuickTime' ) {
                    var mime = $( image ).attr( 'mime' );
                    //Width and height have like 3 error checks to make sure they don't have non-valid width and height attributes (because of browser silliness)
                    var width = ($(image).attr('wdth') != undefined && $(image).attr('wdth') != "undefined" && $(image).attr('wdth') != "-1") ? $(image).attr('wdth') : MAXWIDTH;
                    var height = ($(image).attr('hght') != undefined && $(image).attr('hght') != "undefined" && $(image).attr('wdth') != "-1") ? $(image).attr('hght') : MAXHEIGHT;

                    if ( width > MAXWIDTH ) {
                        height = ( MAXWIDTH / width ) * height;
                        width = MAXWIDTH;
                    }

                    if ( height > MAXHEIGHT ) { // if height still exceeds 480
                        width = ( MAXHEIGHT / height ) * width;
                        height = MAXHEIGHT;
                    }

                    width = Math.round( width );
                    height = Math.round( height );

                        if ( vidType == 'file' ) {
                            var type = getFileType( src ).toLowerCase();
                            var elem = '<video width="'+width+'" height="'+height+'" >';
                            if( !mime ) {
                                return null;
                            }
                            elem+='<source type="'+mime+'" src="'+src+'"/>';
                            elem+='<object width="'+width+'" height="'+height+'" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" data="plugins/MediaElement/build/flashmediaelement.swf">'
                                    +'<param name="movie" value="flash/flashmediaelement.swf" />'
                                    +'<param name="flashvars" value="controls=true&file='+src+'" />'
                                    +'<!-- Image fall back for non-HTML5 browser with JavaScript turned off and no Flash player installed -->'
                                    +'<img width="'+width+'" height="'+height+'" alt="Here we are" title="No video playback capabilities"/>'
                                +'</object>'
                            +'</video>';
                            return elem;
                        } else if ( vidType == "QuickTime" ) { //Embed a QuickTime player
                            var qtEmbed = "<OBJECT CLASSID=\"clsid:02BF25D5-8C17-4B23-BC80-D3488ABDDC6B\"" +
                                        "CODEBASE=\"http://www.apple.com/qtactivex/qtplugin.cab\"" +
                                        "HEIGHT=" + height + "\"" +
                                        " WIDTH=" + width +
                                        ">" +

                                        "<PARAM NAME=\"src\" VALUE=\"" + src + "\" >" +

                                        "<EMBED " +
                                        "SRC=\"" + src + "\"" +
                                        "HEIGHT=" + height + " WIDTH=" + width + " " +
                                        "SCALE=\"tofit\"" + " " +
                                        "TYPE=\"video/quicktime\"" +
                                        "PLUGINSPAGE=\"http://www.apple.com/quicktime/download/\"" +
                                        "/>" +

                                    "</OBJECT>"
                            return qtEmbed;
                        }
                } else if ( vidType == 'youtube' ) { // Youtube of Vimeo
                    var id = extractYoutubeID(src);
                    return '<iframe width="300" height="300" src="http://www.youtube.com/embed/'+id+'" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen></iframe>';
                } else if ( vidType == 'vimeo' ) {
                    var id = extractVimeoID(src);
                    return '<iframe width="300" height="300" src="http://player.vimeo.com/video/'+id+'" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen></iframe>';
                }
                return null;
            }

            /**
                * Generates the HTML for an audio element
                * @param image The visible image that represents the embeded media
                * @returns The HTML for the audio
                */
            function createAudioElement ( image ) {

                var src = $(image).attr('mediaSrc');
                src += '&downloadType=stream';
                var mime = $(image).attr('mime');
                if( !mime ) {
                    return null;
                }
                return '<audio type="'+mime+'" src="'+src+'" preload="none"></audio>';
            }

            /**
                * Plays whatever is in the Media Popup
                */
            function playCurrentMedia () {
                var browser = browserDetect(); //Sniff used browser
                var playerFeatures = ['playpause','current','duration','tracks','volume']
                if(browser != 'safari'){
                    playerFeatures.push( 'fullscreen' );
                }

                $( '#mediaViewer div.mediaContent' ).find( 'audio,video' ).mediaelementplayer({
                    // if the <video width> is not specified, this is the default
                    defaultVideoWidth: MAXWIDTH,
                    // if the <video height> is not specified, this is the default
                    defaultVideoHeight: MAXHEIGHT,
                    // if set, overrides <video width>
                    videoWidth: -1,
                    // if set, overrides <video height>
                    videoHeight: -1,
                    // width of audio player
                    audioWidth: 200,
                    // height of audio player
                    audioHeight: 30,
                    // initial volume when the player starts
                    startVolume: 0.7,
                    // useful for <audio> player loops
                    loop: false,
                    // enables Flash and Silverlight to resize to content size
                    enableAutosize: true,
                    // the order of controls you want on the control bar (and other plugins below)
                    features: playerFeatures,
                    // automatically selects a <track> element
                    startLanguage: '',
                    // a list of languages to auto-translate via Google
                    translations: [],
                    // a dropdownlist of automatic translations
                    translationSelector: false,
                    // key for tranlsations
                    googleApiKey: ''
                });
//                    .bind('play', function() {
//                        if(this.tagName == 'AUDIO' || this.tagName == 'audio') { //Audio does not have any loading indicator, so we make one
//                            $(this).parents('div.mejs-container').hide()
//                            .after('<img src="images/ajax-loader.gif" style="width:210px" />');
//                        }
//                    }).bind('playing', function() {
//                        if(this.tagName == 'AUDIO' || this.tagName == 'audio') {
//                            $(this).parents('div.mejs-container').next('img').remove().end().show();
//                        }
//                    });
            }

            /**
                * Searches the user submission for the Youtube video ID
                * @param link The user's input for the Youtube link/id
                * @return the video ID
                */
            function extractYoutubeID( link ) {
                if( link.indexOf( 'youtube' ) >= 0 || link.indexOf( 'youtu.be' ) >= 0 ) {
                    var queryStart = link.indexOf('?');
                    var idStart = link.indexOf('v=', queryStart);
                    if( queryStart > 0 && idStart > 0 ) {
                        // Search for the ID in the query
                        var idEnd = link.indexOf('&', idStart); // Exclude the rest of the query if it exists
                        idEnd = ( idEnd >=0 ) ? idEnd : link.length;
                        if(idStart+2 < idEnd)
                            return link.substring(idStart+2, idEnd);
                    } else {
                        // The ID is the last part of the url
                        idStart = link.lastIndexOf('/');
                        var idEnd = link.indexOf('?', idStart); // Exclude the query, if it exists
                        idEnd = ( idEnd >=0 ) ? idEnd : link.length;
                        return link.substring(idStart+1, idEnd);
                    }
                } else {
                    // Not a link, so must be the video ID
                    return link;
                }
            }

            /**
                * Searches the user submission for the Vimeo video ID
                * @param link The user's input for the Vimeo link/id
                * @return the video ID
                */
            function extractVimeoID( link ) {
                if( link.indexOf( 'vimeo' ) >= 0 ) {
                    // The ID is the last part of the url
                    var idStart = link.lastIndexOf('/');
                    var idEnd = link.indexOf('?', idStart); // Exclude the query, if it exists
                    idEnd = ( idEnd >=0 ) ? idEnd : link.length;
                    return link.substring(idStart+1, idEnd);
                } else {
                    // Not a link, so must be the video ID
                    return link;
                }
            }

            /**
                * Helper function for finding a substring inside a string
                */
            function strstr ( haystack, needle, bool ) {
                // Finds first occurrence of a string within another
                //
                // version: 1103.1210
                // discuss at: http://phpjs.org/functions/strstr    // +   original by: Kevin van Zonneveld (http://kevin.vanzonneveld.net)
                // +   bugfixed by: Onno Marsman
                // +   improved by: Kevin van Zonneveld (http://kevin.vanzonneveld.net)
                // *     example 1: strstr(Kevin van Zonneveld, van);
                // *     returns 1: van Zonneveld    // *     example 2: strstr(Kevin van Zonneveld, van, true);
                // *     returns 2: Kevin 
                // *     example 3: strstr(name@example.com, @);
                // *     returns 3: @example.com
                // *     example 4: strstr(name@example.com, @, true);    // *     returns 4: name
                var pos = 0;

                haystack += "";
                pos = haystack.indexOf(needle); if (pos == -1) {
                    return false;
                } else {
                    if (bool) {
                        return haystack.substr(0, pos);
                    } else {
                        return haystack.slice(pos);
                    }
                }
            }
  </script>
